# 轻小说 2018~2020 NPM、PYPI、DockerHub 备份

## 爱的魔法 - 筑地俊彦 - 20200306


### Docker

```
docker pull apachecn0/ai-de-mofa-zhu-dijunyan-20200306
docker run -tid -p <port>:80 apachecn0/ai-de-mofa-zhu-dijunyan-20200306
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### PYPI

```
pip install ai-de-mofa-zhu-dijunyan-20200306
ai-de-mofa-zhu-dijunyan-20200306 <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### NPM

```
npm install -g ai-de-mofa-zhu-dijunyan-erlingerlinglingsanlingliu
ai-de-mofa-zhu-dijunyan-erlingerlinglingsanlingliu <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```
